			<script type="text/javascript">
			var src ="//in.bmscdn.com/iedb/movies/images/website/banner/large/june-et00096265-09-02-2019-06-59-34.jpg", imgSrc = "//in.bmscdn.com/iedb/movies/images/website/poster/large/june-et00096265-09-02-2019-06-59-34.jpg";			function fnChangeUrl(pathName) {
				try {
					var myURL = window.location.pathname.substr(0, window.location.pathname.indexOf("movies"));
					window.location = myURL+"movies/"+pathName;
				} catch(e) {
					BMS.Misc.fnErr({ fnName : "fnChangeUrl", err : e });
				}
			}

		<div id="criticReview_" class="__reviewer-text">
			<span itemprop="description" >In a recent interview, the makers were asked whether this is the Premam of Rajisha Vijayan. Well after watching the film I would say it is more of a Dear Zindagi of Rajisha Vijayan. The movie is from the female perspective and never tries to ridicule its male characters and I would say that is something some of the other film makers should look at and learn from these debutants.</span>
			<a href="https://lensmenreviews.com/june-malayalam-movie-review-2019/" class="__read-review-link" target="_blank">...Read full review</a>
		</div>
	</div>
</div>                        </div>
                                            </div>
